Next is to make a linear regression on the scatterplot. The function lm() works for this. 

BEFORE THE REGRESSION YOU SHOULD BE GUESSTIMATING THE RELATIONSHIP AND THE SLOPE AND Y-INTERCEPT. I'D LIKE TO SEE THAT IN YOUR CODE.


<!-- rnb-text-end -->

```r
```r
model_pgr <- lm(plant.growth.rate ~ soil.moisture.content, data = Growth_Rate)

  geom_point() +
  geom_smooth(method = 'lm') +
  ylab(\Plant Growth Rate (mm/week\) +
  theme_bw()
